| <span data-ttu-id="de8ca-689">Ввод</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="de8ca-689">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="de8ca-690">Значение</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="de8ca-690">Value</span></span> |
